name:J‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äça‚Äçt‚Äçh‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äç ‚ÄçS‚Äçe‚Äçt‚Äçh
info:1 King Bed Classic
info:Stayed in March 2023
info:Business travelers
info:2 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 20, 2023
msg:I was among the first Western business travelers to come back to China after the reopening and needed to visit a company near the convention center. Hotel was spectacular, service was outstanding, location was perfect, rooms were clean with great features, business lounge was top notch, and best of all was the breakfast. I had a chance to talk to Richard, the executive lead chef and he went way beyond the call to make the breakfast offerings truly the best I have experienced at any top hotel anywhere. Because I was one of the first Western business travelers after the reopening, I had lots of great hotel options at very reasonable prices (since vacancies were so high) and I am so glad I picked the Intercontinental. Food is very important to me and I had seen other reviews about the great food here. Truly the best, and Richard deserves huge accolades for not only the quality, but the variety. I could not have asked for more. In addition, all of the staff (front desk, concierge, etc) were over the top great. Location is great for Hongqiao Airport and the train station and the Shanghai metro stop is just a quick walk from the front door of the hotel. And the metro stop that services the hotel allows for direct travel (with or without interchange) all over Shanghai. I tend to use taxis or ride apps in China, but the Shanghai metro bypasses traffic and is THE way to go during rush hour. I will be back to this hotel for sure. It gets a 10 out of 10 in all categories for me!
